Color barsâ=â-log<sub>10</sub>(p-value). <b>c</b>, Density of m<sup>6</sup>A marks in the genic region, 5Ê¹ and 3Ê¹ UTR of ethe xpressed genes in the fiber (red) and leaf (green). Studentâs <i>t</i>-test was used to compare between m<sup>6</sup>A immuno-precipitated and fragmented (control) RNA reads with single (*) and triple (***) asterisks indicating statistical significance levels of Pâ&lt;â0.05 and &lt;0.001, respectively. <b>d</b>, Expression levels (<i>y</i> axis) of the genes with m<sup>6</sup>A peaks in the leaf (161 genes) and fiber (1,205 genes) (green), relative to all homoeologous genes (red). Studentâs <i>t</i>-test was used to compare between m<sup>6</sup>A-associated genes and all homoeologous genes with double (**) and triple (***) asterisks indicating statistical significance levels of Pâ&lt;â0.01 and &lt;0.001, respectively.
                          <a data-track="click" data-track-label="link" data-track-action="supplementary material anchor" href="/articles/s41588-020-0614-5#MOESM15">Source data</a>
                        </p></div></div><div class="c-article-supplementary__item js-c-reading-companion-figures-item" data-test="supp-item" id="Fig13"><h3 class="c-article-supplementary__title u-h3"><a class="print-link" data-track="click" data-track-action="view supplementary info" data-track-label="link" data-test="supp-info-link" href="/articles/s41588-020-0614-5/figures/13" data-supp-info-image="//media.springernature.com/lw685/springer-static/esm/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41588-020-0614-5/MediaObjects/41588_2020_614_Fig13_ESM.jpg">Extended Data Fig. 9 Recombination rate distribution in <i>G. hirsutum</i> and inheritance of haplotype blocks in two breeding populations.</a></h3><div class="c-article-supplementary__description" data-component="thumbnail-container"><p><b>a</b>, Recombination rate distribution between A and D subgenomes. The recombination bins are based on overlapping 5-Mb windows. The dashed grey lines indicate 50% of individuals recombined in the window. The pale blue polygons link syntenic regions. The <i>x</i> axis is scaled independently for each homoeologous chromosome. <b>b</b>, Linkage disequilibrium heatmap of chromosome A08 of the <i>G. hirsutum</i>X<i>G. mustelinum</i> BC<sub>2</sub>F<sub>1</sub> population. Genotypes of 18 lines each representative of one family, two parents, and F<sub>1</sub> are shown using the CottonSNP63K array (top panel). Red, yellow, and blue colors show the genotypes homozygous for <i>G. hirsutum</i>, homozygous for <i>G. mustelinum</i>, and heterozygous for both species, respectively. Heatmap (bottom panel) consists of equidistant tiles that indicate linkage disequilibrium as determined by a normalized coefficient of linkage disequilibrium (<i>D</i>â) between pairs of markers. Markers corresponding to SNP positions above the heatmap are congruent to the introgressed genotypes (<i>x</i> axis). <b>c</b>, Linkage disequilibrium heatmap of chromosome A08 of the <i>G. hirsutum</i>X<i>G. tomentosum</i> BC<sub>3</sub>F<sub>1</sub> population. Genotypes of 33 lines each representative of one family, two parents, and F<sub>1</sub> are shown using the CottonSNP63K array (top panel). Red, yellow, and blue colors show the genotypes homozygous for <i>G. hirsutum</i>, homozygous for <i>G. tomentosum</i>, and heterozygous for both species, respectively. Heatmap (bottom panel) consists of equidistant tiles that indicate linkage disequilibrium as determined by a normalized coefficient of linkage disequilibrium (<i>D</i>â) between pairs of markers. Markers corresponding to SNP positions above the heatmap are congruent to the introgressed genotypes (<i>x</i> axis).
                          <a data-track="click" data-track-label="link" data-track-action="supplementary material anchor" href="/articles/s41588-020-0614-5#MOESM16">Source data</a>
                        </p></div></div><div class="c-article-supplementary__item js-c-reading-companion-figures-item" data-test="supp-item" id="Fig14"><h3 class="c-article-supplementary__title u-h3"><a class="print-link" data-track="click" data-track-action="view supplementary info" data-track-label="link" data-test="supp-info-link" href="/articles/s41588-020-0614-5/figures/14" data-supp-info-image="//media.springernature.com/lw685/springer-static/esm/art%3A10.1038%2Fs41588-020-0614-5/MediaObjects/41588_2020_614_Fig14_ESM.jpg">Extended Data Fig. 10 Correlation of DNA methylation levels and chromatin connecting sites and intensities with recombination cold (haplotype block) and hot (no block) spots.</a></h3><div class="c-article-supplementary__description" data-component="thumbnail-container"><p><b>a</b>, Average percentage (%) of CG (circle), CHG (triangle), and CHH (cross) methylation in the recombination hot (red) and cold (blue) spots between Gb (<i>y</i> axis) and Gh (<i>x</i> axis), with an enlarged image showing CHH methylation levels. Pearson correlation coefficient is 0.994. <b>b</b>, Average methylation percentage (<i>y</i> axis) of the recombination spots in different cross in CG, CHG, and CHH sites (<i>x</i> axis). Colors indicate recombination hot and cold spots in the three interspecific crosses GhXGbF<sub>2</sub> (red and blue), GmXGhBC<sub>1</sub>F<sub>1</sub> (pink and light blue), and GtXGhBC<sub>1</sub>F<sub>1</sub> (white and black), respectively. ANOVA was used for statistical tests with ingle (*), double (**), and triple (***) asterisks indicating statistical significance levels of P-value&lt;0.001, &lt;1e-5, and &lt;1e-10, respectively. <b>c</b>, Chromatin interaction matrices show correlation of chromatin connecting intensity (<i>y</i> axis, cutoff &gt;5) with average chromatin connecting numbers (<i>x</i> axis, 20-Kb window) of recombination hot (red) and cold (blue) spots in the three interspecific crosses, GhXGbF<sub>2</sub> (circles), GmXGhBC<sub>1</sub>F<sub>1</sub> (triangles), GtXGhBC<sub>1</sub>F<sub>1</sub> (squares). Pearson correlation coefficient is -0.874 with triple (***) asterisks indicating the statistical significance level of P-value&lt;1e-10 (Studentâs <i>t</i>-test). <b>d</b>, Comparison of Hi-C interaction matrix (log2-intensity) in chromosome A08 of the GbXGhF<sub>2</sub> cross, consisting of recombination hot (red) and cold spots (blue). Locations for one hot spot and two cold spots are shown. <b>e</b>, Zoom-in images of two cold and one hot spots in Hi-C interaction matrix (log2 intensity) in chromosome A08, consisting of recombination hot (red) and cold spots (blue), with CG (black), CHG (blue), and CHH (red) methylation densities (100-kb sliding windows). Values at the top of the heatmap represent Hi-C window size (20-kb) and genomic locations (Mb). Gh: <i>G. hirsutum</i>; Gb: <i>G. barbadense</i>; Gt: <i>G. tomentosum</i>; Gm: <i>G. mustelinum</i>.

                <ul data-test="author-list"
                    class="c-article-further-reading__authors-list js-list-authors-3 js-etal-collapsed" data-component-authors-activator="authors-list"
                    id="authors-3">
                  <li><span

              <p class="c-article-further-reading__journal-title" id="journal-name-3">
                <i>Theoretical and Applied Genetics</i>
                (2021)
              </p>
            </li>
